function CreateInstance(cls,props)
	inst = Instance.new(cls)
	for i,v in pairs(props) do
		inst[i] = v
	end
	return inst
end

--PreExecute

--Unicode Generation
local serial = ""
for i = 1, 7 do
	serial = serial .. string.char(math.random(100,150))
	STKv7_Engine_Edtion.Name = serial
end

function Loading()----Remove this section to use the gui on any gamemode
	print("Checking Requirments") 
end 
if game.PlaceId == 2092166489 then
	Loading() print("Classic Mode Loaded")
elseif  game.PlaceId == 5740483929 then 
	Loading() print("Classic Hard Mode Loaded")
elseif game.PlaceId == 3182083477 then 
	Loading() print("Classic Extreme Mode Loaded")else 
	game.Players.LocalPlayer:Kick("Wrong Gamemode")
	wait(1) firetouchinterest(Player.Character,game:GetService("Workspace").PACKAPUNCH.GUI, 0) 
end---------------------------------------------------------------------

--Notfiy
function Notify(NT, NTT)
	game.StarterGui:SetCore('SendNotification', {
		Title = NT, 
		Text = NTT}) end
Notify('Gui Loaded', 'Beginning To Load Scripts ')

	if v.name == "AntiOoB" then v:destroy() end end

--Functions

--BringGuns
function BringGun(Gunname)
	for _,GunGiver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if GunGiver.name == "PUT THE WEAPON IN THIS BRICK" 
			and GunGiver.Parent.Parent.name == Gunname then 
			print(GunGiver.Parent.Parent.name) 
			firetouchinterest(Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart,GunGiver, 0) 
		end end end  

--Beta Verison
--for _,GunGiver in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Weapons:GetDescendants()) do 
--if GunGiver.name == "Hitbox"  then 
--	print(GunGiver.Parent.name) 
--firetouchinterest(Humanoid,GunGiver, 0) 
--end end

--BringItems
function BringItem(RoomName)
	for _,ItemGiver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if ItemGiver.name == "PUT THIS IN THE WEAPON" 
			and ItemGiver.Parent.Parent.name == RoomName then 
			print(ItemGiver.Parent.Parent.name) 
			firetouchinterest(Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart,ItemGiver.Parent, 0) 
		end end end  

--Bring Card
function KeyCard(RoomName)
	for _,CardReciver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if CardReciver.name == "Card" 
			and CardReciver.Parent.name == RoomName then 
			firetouchinterest(Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart,CardReciver, 0) 
		end end end  

--Bring Vest
function EventItems(RoomName)
	for _,EventGiver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if EventGiver.name == "Giver" 
			and EventGiver.Parent.name == RoomName then 
			firetouchinterest(Humanoid,EventGiver, 0) 
		end end end  
--Teleport
function PlayerTp(x,y,z) 
	Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(x,y,z)) end

--GunTeleport
function GunTp(Gunname)
	for _,GunReciver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if GunReciver.name == "PUT THE WEAPON IN THIS BRICK" 
			and GunReciver.Parent.Parent.name == Gunname then 
			Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = GunReciver.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(1,4,1)) 
		end end end  

--ItemTeleport
function ItemTp(RoomName)
	for _,ItemReciver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if ItemReciver.name == "PUT THIS IN THE WEAPON" 
			and ItemReciver.Parent.Parent.name == RoomName then 
			Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = ItemReciver.Parent.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(1,4,1)) 
		end end end  
--Slider For Bullet COunt
function SlideV(Framv,Buttvn)
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local Dragging = false

	Buttvn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		Dragging = true
	end)
	UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function()
		if Dragging then
			local MousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()+Vector2.new(0,36)
			local RelPos = MousePos-Framv.AbsolutePosition
			local Precent = math.clamp(RelPos.X/Framv.AbsoluteSize.X,0,1)
			Buttvn.Position = UDim2.new(Precent,0,0.5,0)
			for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
				if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'ammo')then
					v.bullet_count = Precent*100 end end end end)
	UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
			Dragging = false end end) end
SlideV(TSBulletCount,TSBBulleta)

--Slider For WS
function SlidePv(Framv,Buttvn)
	local UserInputService = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local Dragging = false

	Buttvn.MouseButton1Down:Connect(function()
		Dragging = true
	end)
	UserInputService.InputChanged:Connect(function()
		if Dragging then
			local MousePos = UserInputService:GetMouseLocation()+Vector2.new(0,36)
			local RelPos = MousePos-Framv.AbsolutePosition
			local Precent = math.clamp(RelPos.X/Framv.AbsoluteSize.X,0,1)
			Buttvn.Position = UDim2.new(Precent,0,0.5,0) 
			----------------------------------
			local walkSpeed = Precent * 100 + 20
			local tables = getrawmetatable(game)
			setreadonly(tables, false)
			local oldindex = tables.__index
			tables.__index = newcclosure(function(self,ass)
				if ass == "WalkSpeed" then
					return 16 end
				return oldindex(self,ass)
			end)
			game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = walkSpeed
			UserInputService.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
				if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then
					Dragging = false end end) end end) end


SlidePv(TSWalk,TSBWalkia)

---------------------Create
UIAspectRatioConstraint = CreateInstance('UIAspectRatioConstraint',{Name='UIAspectRatioConstraint', Parent=ColourWheel})
UIAspectRatioConstraint = CreateInstance('UIAspectRatioConstraint',{Name='UIAspectRatioConstraint', Parent=DarknessPicker})

--Create Color Wheel
function ColorTrigger()
	--Color Wheel

	local uis = game:GetService("UserInputService")
	local buttonDown = false
	local movingSlider = false
	local function updateColour(centreOfWheel)
		local colourPickerCentre = Vector2.new(
			ColourWheel.Picker.AbsolutePosition.X + (ColourWheel.Picker.AbsoluteSize.X/2),
			ColourWheel.Picker.AbsolutePosition.Y + (ColourWheel.Picker.AbsoluteSize.Y/2))
		local h = (math.pi - math.atan2(colourPickerCentre.Y - centreOfWheel.Y, colourPickerCentre.X - centreOfWheel.X)) / (math.pi * 2)
		local s = (centreOfWheel - colourPickerCentre).Magnitude / (ColourWheel.AbsoluteSize.X/2)
		local v = math.abs((Slider.AbsolutePosition.Y - DarknessPicker.AbsolutePosition.Y) / DarknessPicker.AbsoluteSize.Y - 1)
		local hsv = Color3.fromHSV(math.clamp(h, 0, 1), math.clamp(s, 0, 1), math.clamp(v, 0, 1))

		GameType.TextColor3=hsv
		MenuType.TextColor3=hsv
		Verison_E.TextColor3=hsv
		--Toggles
		T_GiveAllGuns.TextColor3=hsv
		T_DemiGod.TextColor3=hsv
		T_Esp.TextColor3=hsv
		T_FCD.TextColor3=hsv
		T_FOD.TextColor3=hsv
		T_InfiniteAmmo.TextColor3=hsv
		T_FullAuto.TextColor3=hsv
		T_HGunM.TextColor3=hsv
		T_INF.TextColor3=hsv
		T_LGunM.TextColor3=hsv
		T_MGundM.TextColor3=hsv
		T_Fog.TextColor3=hsv

		T_Jump_I.TextColor3=hsv
		T_Nocplip.TextColor3=hsv
		BackRound.ImageColor3 = hsv

		DarknessPicker.UIGradient.Color = ColorSequence.new{
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(0, hsv), 
			ColorSequenceKeypoint.new(1, Color3.new(0, 0, 0))}end
	ColourWheel.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
		buttonDown = true
	end)
	DarknessPicker.MouseButton1Down:connect(function()
		movingSlider = true
	end)
	uis.InputEnded:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 then return end
		buttonDown = false
		movingSlider = false end)
	uis.InputChanged:Connect(function(input)
		if input.UserInputType ~= Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement then return end
		local mousePos = uis:GetMouseLocation() - Vector2.new(0, game:GetService("GuiService"):GetGuiInset().Y)
		local centreOfWheel = Vector2.new(ColourWheel.AbsolutePosition.X + (ColourWheel.AbsoluteSize.X/2), ColourWheel.AbsolutePosition.Y + (ColourWheel.AbsoluteSize.Y/2))
		local distanceFromWheel = (mousePos - centreOfWheel).Magnitude
		if distanceFromWheel <= ColourWheel.AbsoluteSize.X/2 and buttonDown then
			Picker.Position = UDim2.new(0, mousePos.X - ColourWheel.AbsolutePosition.X, 0, mousePos.Y - ColourWheel.AbsolutePosition.Y)
		elseif movingSlider then
			Slider.Position = UDim2.new(Slider.Position.X.Scale, 0, 0, 
				math.clamp(
					mousePos.Y - DarknessPicker.AbsolutePosition.Y, 
					0, 
					DarknessPicker.AbsoluteSize.Y))	end
		updateColour(centreOfWheel)end) end

--Scripts
function DemiGod(Frame)
	local stationaryrespawn = false
	local needsrespawning = false
	local haspos = false
	local pos = CFrame.new()
	function StatRespawn(inputObject, gameProcessedEvent)
		if inputObject.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.N and gameProcessedEvent == false then        
			stationaryrespawn = not stationaryrespawn end end
	game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:connect(StatRespawn)
	game:GetService('RunService').Stepped:connect(function()
		if stationaryrespawn == false and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Humanoid.Health == 0 
			and Frame.Text == OnE then
			if haspos == false then
				pos = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
				haspos = true end
			needsrespawning = true end
		if needsrespawning == true then
			game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = pos
		end end)
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:connect(function()
		wait(0.6)
		needsrespawning = false
		haspos = false end)
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:connect(function()
		wait(0.1)
		needsrespawning = false
		haspos = false end)
	game.Players.LocalPlayer.CharacterAdded:connect(function()
		wait(0.1)
		needsrespawning = false
		haspos = false end) end

function InfiniteAmmo()
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'ammo')then
			v.ammo = math.huge
			v.stored_ammo = math.huge
		end end end 

function GiveAmmo()
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'ammo')then
			v.stored_ammo = v.max_stored
		end end end

function SemiInvisble() 
	Local = game:GetService('Players').LocalPlayer
	Char  = Local.Character
	touched,tpdback = false, false
	Local.CharacterAdded:connect(function(char)
		if script.Disabled ~= true and SInvinisbleM.TextStrokeColor3 == Green then
			wait(.25)
			loc = Char.HumanoidRootPart.Position
			Char:MoveTo(box.Position + Vector3.new(0,.5,0)) end end)
	game:GetService('UserInputService').InputBegan:connect(function(key)
		if key.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Equals then
			if script.Disabled ~= true then
				script.Disabled = true end end end)
	box = Instance.new('Part',workspace)
	box.Anchored = true
	box.CanCollide = true
	box.Size = Vector3.new(10,1,10)
	box.Position = Vector3.new(0,10000,0)
	box.Touched:connect(function(part)
		if (part.Parent.Name == Local.Name) then
			if touched == false then
				touched = true
				function apply()
					if script.Disabled ~= true then
						no = Char.HumanoidRootPart:Clone()
						wait(.25)
						Char.HumanoidRootPart:Destroy()
						no.Parent = Char
						Char:MoveTo(loc)
						touched = false  end end
				if Char then apply() end end end end)
	repeat wait() until Char
	loc = Char.HumanoidRootPart.Position
	Char:MoveTo(box.Position + Vector3.new(0,.5,0))end

function GiveAllGuns()
	for _,GunGiver in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if GunGiver.name == "PUT THE WEAPON IN THIS BRICK" 
		then firetouchinterest(Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart,GunGiver, 0) end end end

function GiveDeleteTool()
	local a=Instance.new("Tool")a.RequiresHandle=false;a.Name="Delete"
	local b=game.Players.LocalPlayer;a.Parent=b:WaitForChild("Backpack")local c=b:GetMouse()
	local d=false;local e=Instance.new("SelectionBox")e.Color3=Color3.new(0, 1, 1)e.Parent=b.PlayerGui;
	local c=b:GetMouse()
	local e=Instance.new("SelectionBox")e.Color3=Color3.new(0, 1, 1)e.Parent=b.PlayerGui;e.Name="derp"c.Move:connect(function()if d then local f=c.Target;
			if not f then e.Adornee=nil else if f:IsA("BasePart")then e.Adornee=f else e.Adornee=nil end end end end)
	a.Equipped:Connect(function()d=true end)a.Unequipped:Connect(function()e.Adornee=nil;d=false end)
	a.Activated:Connect(function()if e.Adornee then 
			local g=Instance.new("Explosion")g.Parent=game.Workspace;g.Position=e.Adornee.Position;g.BlastPressure=0;
			local h=Instance.new("Sound")h.SoundId="http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=315775189"h.Parent=game.Workspace;h:Play()e.Adornee:Destroy()e.Adornee=nil end end)
end

function CamaraMode()
	OldPos = game:GetService("Workspace")["Surveillance Cameras"].Triggers.Seat.CFrame
	HoldPos = Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame
	wait()
	game:GetService("Workspace")["Surveillance Cameras"].Triggers.Seat.CFrame 
		= game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Torso.CFrame
	wait()
	UserInputService.InputBegan:Connect(function(input, gameProcessed)
		if input.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Keyboard then
			local keyPressed = input.Space
			Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame	= HoldPos    
			game:GetService("Workspace")["Surveillance Cameras"].Triggers.Seat.CFrame = OldPos
		end end) end 

function Aimbot(TType,DistanceE) --Settings Here, -- Not mine, just slightly edited

	game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
		Title = "AIMBOT",
		Text = "Press Left Ctrl"
	}) --
	--game:GetService("StarterGui"):SetCore("SendNotification", {
	--  Title = "ESP NAME",
	--  Text = "Press Left Alt"
	--})
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'inaccuracy')then
			v.inaccuracy = 0.000001
		end end
	ZOMBIE  = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	MOUSE   = ZOMBIE:GetMouse()
	CC      = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera
	ENABLED      = TType
	ESP_ENABLED  = false

	_G.FREE_FOR_ALL = true
	_G.BIND        = 50
	--_G.ESP_BIND    = 52
	_G.CHANGE_AIM  = 'gfdkdfvdgfdgccv'
	_G.AIM_AT = 'Head'

	MOBLESS = game:GetService("Workspace").Killers
	ESPMOBLESS = game:GetService("Workspace").Killers
	wait(1)
	function GetNearestPlayerToMouse()
		local ZOMBIES      = {}
		local ZOMBIE_HOLD  = {}
		local DISTANCES    = {}
		for i, v in pairs(MOBLESS:GetDescendants()) do------- 
			if v ~= ZOMBIE then 
				table.insert(ZOMBIES, v)
			end
		end
		for i, v in pairs(ZOMBIES) do 
			if _G.FREE_FOR_ALL == false then
				if v and (v.Character) ~= nil and v.TeamColor ~= ZOMBIE.TeamColor then
					local AIM = v.Character:FindFirstChild(_G.AIM_AT)
					if AIM ~= nil then
						local DISTANCE                 = (AIM.Position - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude
						local RAY                      = Ray.new(game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p, (MOUSE.Hit.p - CC.CoordinateFrame.p).unit * DISTANCE)
						local HIT,POS                  = game.Workspace:FindPartOnRay(RAY, game.Workspace)
						local DIFF                     = math.floor((POS - AIM.Position).magnitude)
						ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i]       = {}
						ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i].dist  = DISTANCE
						ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i].plr   = v
						ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i].diff  = DIFF
						table.insert(DISTANCES, DIFF)
					end
				end
			elseif _G.FREE_FOR_ALL == true then
				local AIM = v:FindFirstChild(_G.AIM_AT)
				if AIM ~= nil then
					local DISTANCE                 = (AIM.Position - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p).magnitude
					local RAY                      = Ray.new(game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p, (MOUSE.Hit.p - CC.CoordinateFrame.p).unit * DISTANCE)
					local HIT,POS                  = game.Workspace:FindPartOnRay(RAY, game.Workspace)
					local DIFF                     = math.floor((POS - AIM.Position).magnitude)
					ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i]       = {}
					ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i].dist  = DISTANCE
					ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i].plr   = v
					ZOMBIE_HOLD[v.Name .. i].diff  = DIFF
					table.insert(DISTANCES, DIFF)
					--print(v.name "found")
				end end end
		if unpack(DISTANCES) == nil then
			return false end
		local L_DISTANCE = math.floor(math.min(unpack(DISTANCES)))
		if L_DISTANCE > DistanceE then
			return false end
		for i, v in pairs(ZOMBIE_HOLD) do
			if v.diff == L_DISTANCE then return v.plr end end return false end

	GUI_MAIN                           = Instance.new('ScreenGui', game.CoreGui)
	GUI_TARGET                         = Instance.new('TextLabel', GUI_MAIN)
	GUI_AIM_AT                         = Instance.new('TextLabel', GUI_MAIN)

	GUI_MAIN.Name                      = 'AIMBOT'

	GUI_TARGET.Size                    = UDim2.new(0,200,0,30)
	GUI_TARGET.BackgroundTransparency  = 0.5
	GUI_TARGET.BackgroundColor         = BrickColor.new('Fossil')
	GUI_TARGET.BorderSizePixel         = 0
	GUI_TARGET.Position                = UDim2.new(0.5,-100,0,0)
	GUI_TARGET.Text                    = 'AIMBOT : OFF'
	GUI_TARGET.TextColor3              = Color3.new(1,1,1)
	GUI_TARGET.TextStrokeTransparency  = 1
	GUI_TARGET.TextWrapped             = true
	GUI_TARGET.FontSize                = 'Size24'
	GUI_TARGET.Font                    = 'SourceSansBold'

	GUI_AIM_AT.Size                    = UDim2.new(0,200,0,20)
	GUI_AIM_AT.BackgroundTransparency  = 0.5
	GUI_AIM_AT.BackgroundColor         = BrickColor.new('Fossil')
	GUI_AIM_AT.BorderSizePixel         = 0
	GUI_AIM_AT.Position                = UDim2.new(0.5,-100,0,30)
	GUI_AIM_AT.Text                    = 'AIMING : HEAD'
	GUI_AIM_AT.TextColor3              = Color3.new(1,1,1)
	GUI_AIM_AT.TextStrokeTransparency  = 1
	GUI_AIM_AT.TextWrapped             = true
	GUI_AIM_AT.FontSize                = 'Size18'
	GUI_AIM_AT.Font                    = 'SourceSansBold'

	local TRACK = false

	function CREATE(BASE, TEAM)
		local ESP_MAIN                   = Instance.new('BillboardGui', ZOMBIE.PlayerGui)
		local ESP_DOT                    = Instance.new('Frame', ESP_MAIN)
		local ESP_NAME                   = Instance.new('TextLabel', ESP_MAIN)

		ESP_MAIN.Name                    = 'ESP'
		ESP_MAIN.Adornee                 = BASE
		ESP_MAIN.AlwaysOnTop             = true
		ESP_MAIN.ExtentsOffset           = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0)
		ESP_MAIN.Size                    = UDim2.new(0, 5, 0, 5)

		ESP_DOT.Name                     = 'DOT'
		ESP_DOT.BackgroundColor          = BrickColor.new('Toothpaste')
		ESP_DOT.BackgroundTransparency   = 0.3
		ESP_DOT.BorderSizePixel          = 0
		ESP_DOT.Position                 = UDim2.new(-0.5, 0, -0.5, 0)
		ESP_DOT.Size                     = UDim2.new(2, 0, 2, 0)
		ESP_DOT.Visible                  = true
		ESP_DOT.ZIndex                   = 10

		ESP_NAME.Name                    = 'NAME'
		ESP_NAME.BackgroundColor3        = Color3.new(255, 255, 255)
		ESP_NAME.BackgroundTransparency  = 1
		ESP_NAME.BorderSizePixel         = 0
		ESP_NAME.Position                = UDim2.new(0, 0, 0, -40)
		ESP_NAME.Size                    = UDim2.new(1, 0, 10, 0)
		ESP_NAME.Visible                 = true
		ESP_NAME.ZIndex                  = 10
		ESP_NAME.Font                    = 'ArialBold'
		ESP_NAME.FontSize                = 'Size14'
		ESP_NAME.Text                    = BASE.Parent.Name:upper()
		ESP_NAME.TextColor               = BrickColor.new('Toothpaste')
	end
	function CLEAR()
		for _,v in pairs(ZOMBIE.PlayerGui:children()) do
			if v.Name == 'ESP' and v:IsA('BillboardGui') then
				v:Destroy()
			end end end
	function FIND()
		CLEAR()
		TRACK = true
		spawn(function()
			while wait() do
				if TRACK then
					CLEAR()
					for i,v in pairs(ESPMOBLESS:GetDescendants()) do
						if v and v:FindFirstChild('Head') then
							if _G.FREE_FOR_ALL == false then
								if v.TeamColor ~= ZOMBIE.TeamColor then
									if v:FindFirstChild('Head') then
										CREATE(v.Head, true)
									end end else
								if v:FindFirstChild('Head') then
									CREATE(v.Head, true)
								end end end end end end wait(1) end) end

	MOUSE.KeyDown:connect(function(KEY)
		KEY = KEY:lower():byte()
		if KEY == _G.BIND then
			ENABLED = true
		end end)
	MOUSE.KeyUp:connect(function(KEY)
		KEY = KEY:lower():byte()
		if KEY == _G.BIND then
			ENABLED = TType
		end end)
	MOUSE.KeyDown:connect(function(KEY)
		KEY = KEY:lower():byte()
		if KEY == _G.ESP_BIND then
			if ESP_ENABLED == false then
				FIND()
				ESP_ENABLED = true
			elseif ESP_ENABLED == true then
				wait()
				CLEAR()
				TRACK = false
				ESP_ENABLED = false
			end end end)
	MOUSE.KeyDown:connect(function(KEY)
		if KEY == _G.CHANGE_AIM then
			if _G.AIM_AT == 'Head' then
				_G.AIM_AT = 'Torso'
				GUI_AIM_AT.Text = 'AIMING : TORSO'
			elseif _G.AIM_AT == 'Torso' then
				_G.AIM_AT = 'Head'
				GUI_AIM_AT.Text = 'AIMING : HEAD'
			end end end)
	game:GetService('RunService').RenderStepped:connect(function()
		if ENABLED then
			local TARGET = GetNearestPlayerToMouse()
			if (TARGET ~= false) then
				local AIM = TARGET:FindFirstChild(_G.AIM_AT)
				if AIM then
					CC.CoordinateFrame = CFrame.new(CC.CoordinateFrame.p, AIM.CFrame.p) end
				GUI_TARGET.Text = 'AIMBOT : '.. TARGET.Name:sub(1, 5)
			else GUI_TARGET.Text = 'AIMBOT : OFF'
			end end end) repeat
		wait()
		if ESP_ENABLED == true then FIND() end
	until ESP_ENABLED == false end

function RemoveDamgers() --game:GetService("Workspace").AREA51.RadioactiveArea.Entrance
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "TouchInterest" and v.parent.name == "Pokey" then
			v:Destroy() end end 
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "Radioactive Damage" then v:Destroy() end end
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "TouchInterest" and v.parent.name == "Kill" then
			v:Destroy() end end 
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "TouchInterest" and v.parent.parent.name == "Deadly" then
			v:Destroy() end end 
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "Toxic" and v.parent.name == "Toxic Water" then
			v:Destroy() end end 
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "TouchInterest" and v.parent.parent.parent.name == "Spikes" then
			v:Destroy() end end 
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "TouchInterest" and v.parent.name == "Entrance" then
			v:Destroy() end end

	for i,v in pairs(workspace.AREA51:GetDescendants()) do 
		if v.name == "TouchInterest" and v.parent.parent.name == "Barbeles" then
			v:Destroy() end end
end

function AntiAfk()
	if game:IsLoaded() ~= true then
		game.Loaded:Wait()
	end
	local Players = game:GetService('Players')
	local s,e = pcall(function()
		local GC = getconnections or get_signal_cons
		if GC then
			for i,v in pairs(GC(Players.LocalPlayer.Idled)) do
				if v["Disable"] then
					v["Disable"](v)
				elseif v["Disconnect"] then
					v["Disconnect"](v) end end
			print("Armed") else
			Notify('Outdated Exploit', 'Script was not executed ')
			script:Destroy()
		end end)
	if not s then warn(e); script:Destroy() end end


function RemoveDoors()
	for i,v in pairs(workspace.Doors:GetDescendants()) do
		if  v:IsA ("Part") and v.name == 'Door' then
			v:Destroy() end end end 

function RemoveFog()
	if T_Fog.Text == OnE then
		game.lighting.FogStart = 10000
		game.lighting.FogEnd = 20000 
	else
		game.lighting.FogStart = 20
		game.lighting.FogEnd = 200 
	end
end

function ReJoinworld() game:GetService("TeleportService"):Teleport(game.PlaceId) end 

function FullAuto()
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'inaccuracy')then
			v.inaccuracy = 0.00001 end end
	for i,m in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(m)=='table'and rawget(m,'ammo')then
			m.shoot_wait = .00000000000001
			m.is_auto = true 
			m.is_burst = false end end end

function LightGunMods()
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'inaccuracy')then
			v.inaccuracy = 0.00001 end end
	for i,m in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(m)=='table'and rawget(m,'ammo')then
			m.shoot_wait = .00000000000001
			m.stored_ammo = 1000
			m.bullet_count = 1
		end end end

function MediumGunMods()
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(v)=='table'and rawget(v,'inaccuracy')then
			v.inaccuracy = 0.00001 end end
	for i,m in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(m)=='table'and rawget(m,'ammo') then
			m.ammo = math.huge
			m.stored_ammo = math.huge
			m.bullet_count = 2
			m.shoot_wait = .000000001
			m.is_auto = true end end end 

function HeavyGunMods()
	for i,v in next,getgc(true)do

			v.inaccuracy = 0.00001 end end
	for i,m in next,getgc(true)do

			m.stored_ammo = math.huge
			m.bullet_count = 90
			m.shoot_wait = .000000001
			m.is_auto = true end end end 

function EspKillers(Frame)
	EspButton = Frame
	local esp_settings = { 
		textsize = 8,
		colour = 255, 45, 30
	}
	local gui = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
	local esp = Instance.new("TextLabel",gui) ---- new instances to make the billboard gui and the textlabel
	gui.Name = "Killer Esp"; ---- properties of the esp
	gui.ResetOnSpawn = false
	gui.AlwaysOnTop = true;
	gui.LightInfluence = 0;
	gui.Size = UDim2.new(1.75, 0, 1.75, 0);
	esp.BackgroundColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255);
	esp.Text = ""
	esp.Size = UDim2.new(0.0001, 0.00001, 0.0001, 0.00001);
	esp.BorderSizePixel = 4;
	esp.BorderColor3 = Color3.new(esp_settings.colour)
	esp.BorderSizePixel = 0
	esp.Font = "Michroma"
	esp.TextSize = esp_settings.textsize
	esp.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(esp_settings.colour) -- text colour
	while Frame.Text == OnE do wait() ---- loops faster than a while loop :)
		for i,v in pairs (Killers:GetDescendants()) do
			if  v ~= game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer and 
				v.name == 'Head'   and
				v:FindFirstChild("Killer Esp")==nil and 
				Frame.Text == OnE
				and v.Parent.Parent.Name == "Killers" then    
				print(v.Parent.Name,"Found")
				esp.Text = v.Parent.Name
				gui:Clone().Parent = v 
			end end end 
	if 	Frame.Text == OffE then
		for i,v in pairs(Killers:GetDescendants()) do 
			if v.name == "Killer Esp" then 
				v:destroy() end end end end 

function NerfKillers()
	while wait(5) do
		for _,t in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Killers:GetDescendants()) do 
			if t:IsA'TouchTransmitter' then t:destroy() end end
		for _,t in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace").Killers:GetDescendants()) do 
			if t:IsA'Tool' then t:destroy() end end end end

function InfiniteJump()
	local Mouse = Player:GetMouse()
	Mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(k)
		if T_Jump_I.text == OnE then
			if k:byte() == 32 then
				Humanoid = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid")
				Humanoid:ChangeState("Jumping")
				wait(0.1)
				Humanoid:ChangeState("Seated")end end end) end

function TeleportTool()
	mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
	tool = Instance.new("Tool")
	tool.RequiresHandle = false
	tool.Name = "Tp Tool"
	tool.Activated:connect(function()
		local pos = mouse.Hit+Vector3.new(0,2.5,0)
		pos = CFrame.new(pos.X,pos.Y,pos.Z)
		game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = pos
	end)tool.Parent = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Backpack end

function firerate(Frame)
	for i,m in next,getgc(true)do
		if type(m)=='table'and rawget(m,'ammo') then
			m.shoot_wait = XBullet
			m.is_auto = true 
			m.bullet_count = 1 end end 
	if Frame.Text == "Low" then XBullet = Save_PBC end
	if Frame.Text == "Medium" then  XBullet = .0000001 end
	if Frame.Text == "High" then  XBullet = NHX end  end

		if MenuD.Name == STKv7_Engine_Edtion.Name  then MenuD:Destroy() end end end

function KillerMassTp()
	while  wait() do
		for i,v in pairs(workspace.Killers:GetDescendants()) do 
			if v:IsA 'Humanoid' then if v.Health > 0 and v.Parent.name ~= "Slenderman" 
					and v.Parent.name ~= "Giant"  
					and v.Parent.name ~= "Jane" then
					Player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame	= v.Parent.Torso.CFrame * CFrame.new(Vector3.new(7,2,1)) 
				else if v == nil then
						PlayerTp(322.9, 511.4, 390.2)  
					end end end  end end end




---------------------Scripts from internet
-- Noclip by Alumark on v3rmilion
function noclipL()
	local noclip = true
	local player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local character = player.Character or player.CharacterAdded:Wait()

	local mouse = player:GetMouse()


	while T_Nocplip.Text == OnE do
		player = game.Players.LocalPlayer
		character = player.Character

		if noclip then
			for _, v in pairs(character:GetDescendants()) do
				pcall(function()
					if v:IsA("BasePart") then
						v.CanCollide = false
					end
				end)
			end
		end

		game:GetService("RunService").Stepped:wait()
	end end


function Birdy()
	repeat wait()
	until game.Players.LocalPlayer and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:findFirstChild("Torso") and game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:findFirstChild("Humanoid")
	local mouse = game.Players.LocalPlayer:GetMouse()
	repeat wait() until mouse
	local plr = game.Players.LocalPlayer
	local torso = plr.Character.Torso
	local flying = true
	local deb = true
	local ctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
	local lastctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
	local maxspeed = 50
	local speed = 0

	function Fly()
		local bg = Instance.new("BodyGyro", torso)
		bg.P = 9e4
		bg.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
		bg.cframe = torso.CFrame
		local bv = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", torso)
		bv.velocity = Vector3.new(0,0.1,0)
		bv.maxForce = Vector3.new(9e9, 9e9, 9e9)
		repeat wait()
			plr.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = true
			if ctrl.l + ctrl.r ~= 0 or ctrl.f + ctrl.b ~= 0 then
				speed = speed+.5+(speed/maxspeed)
				if speed > maxspeed then
					speed = maxspeed
				end
			elseif not (ctrl.l + ctrl.r ~= 0 or ctrl.f + ctrl.b ~= 0) and speed ~= 0 then
				speed = speed-1
				if speed < 0 then
					speed = 0
				end
			end
			if (ctrl.l + ctrl.r) ~= 0 or (ctrl.f + ctrl.b) ~= 0 then
				bv.velocity = ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (ctrl.f+ctrl.b)) + ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.new(ctrl.l+ctrl.r,(ctrl.f+ctrl.b)*.2,0).p) - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p))*speed
				lastctrl = {f = ctrl.f, b = ctrl.b, l = ctrl.l, r = ctrl.r}
			elseif (ctrl.l + ctrl.r) == 0 and (ctrl.f + ctrl.b) == 0 and speed ~= 0 then
				bv.velocity = ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (lastctrl.f+lastctrl.b)) + ((game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.new(lastctrl.l+lastctrl.r,(lastctrl.f+lastctrl.b)*.2,0).p) - game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p))*speed
			else
				bv.velocity = Vector3.new(0,0.1,0)
			end
			bg.cframe = game.Workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * CFrame.Angles(-math.rad((ctrl.f+ctrl.b)*50*speed/maxspeed),0,0)
		until not flying
		ctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		lastctrl = {f = 0, b = 0, l = 0, r = 0}
		speed = 0
		bg:Destroy()
		bv:Destroy()
		plr.Character.Humanoid.PlatformStand = false
	end
	mouse.KeyDown:connect(function(key)
		if key:lower() == "e" then
			if flying then flying = false
			else
				flying = true
				Fly()
			end
		elseif key:lower() == "w" then
			ctrl.f = 1
		elseif key:lower() == "s" then
			ctrl.b = -1
		elseif key:lower() == "a" then
			ctrl.l = -1
		elseif key:lower() == "d" then
			ctrl.r = 1
		end
	end)
	mouse.KeyUp:connect(function(key)
		if key:lower() == "w" then
			ctrl.f = 0
		elseif key:lower() == "s" then
			ctrl.b = 0
		elseif key:lower() == "a" then
			ctrl.l = 0
		elseif key:lower() == "d" then
			ctrl.r = 0
		end
	end)
	Fly() end

function ForceDoorsD(Even) -- Only Loop, Locks all 
	while true do wait()
		for i,v in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
			if  v.Name == "ProximityPrompt" and v.Parent.Name == Even then
				v.MaxActivationDistance = 9999999999
				fireproximityprompt(v,0)
				--renderstep
			end
		end end end

S_QuickMods_MM.MouseButton1Down:connect(function() 
	LightGunMods()
	Aimbot(false,20)
	toggle(T_Esp) wait()
	EspKillers(T_Esp) 
	local walkSpeed = 20
	local tables = getrawmetatable(game)
	setreadonly(tables, false)
	local oldindex = tables.__index
	tables.__index = newcclosure(function(self,ass)
		if ass == "WalkSpeed" then
			return 16 end
		return oldindex(self,ass)
	end) end)

TSFireRateFA.MouseButton1Down:connect(function() 
	if TSFirerate_Label.Text == "Low" then TSFirerate_Label.Text = "Medium" else TSFirerate_Label.Text = "High"
		firerate(TSFirerate_Label)
	end end)

TSFireRateBA.MouseButton1Down:connect(function() 
	if TSFirerate_Label.Text == "High" then TSFirerate_Label.Text = "Medium" else TSFirerate_Label.Text = "Low"
		firerate(TSFirerate_Label)
	end end)
